6389 <section id="_142">

6390

6391 <h2>

6392Changes to This Summary (06/30/2023)</h2>

6393

6394 <div id="_section_142" class="pdq-sections">

6395<p id="_143" tabindex="-1">

6396The PDQ cancer information summaries are reviewed regularly and updated as new information becomes available. This section describes the latest changes made to this summary as of the date above.</p>

6397<p id="_1335" tabindex="-1">

6398Editorial changes were made to this summary.</p>

6399<p id="_disclaimerHP_3" tabindex="-1">

6400This summary is written and maintained by the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq/editorial-boards/adult-treatment" title="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq/editorial-boards/adult-treatment">

6401PDQ Adult Treatment Editorial Board</a>

6402, which is

6403editorially independent of NCI. The summary reflects an independent review of

6404the literature and does not represent a policy statement of NCI or NIH. More

6405information about summary policies and the role of the PDQ Editorial Boards in

6406maintaining the PDQ summaries can be found on the <a href="/types/colorectal/hp/rectal-treatment-pdq#_AboutThis_1">

6407About This PDQ Summary</a>

6408 and <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq" title="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq">

6409PDQ&#174; Cancer Information for Health Professionals</a>

6410 pages.

6411</p>

6412</div>

6413

6414 </section>

6415

6416

6417

6418 <section id="_AboutThis_1">

6419

6420 <h2>

6421About This PDQ Summary</h2>

6422

6423 <div id="_section_AboutThis_1" class="pdq-sections">

6424<section id="_AboutThis_2">

6425<h3 id="_AboutThis_2_toc">

6426Purpose of This Summary</h3>

6427<p id="_AboutThis_3" tabindex="-1">

6428This PDQ cancer information summary for health professionals provides comprehensive, peer-reviewed, evidence-based information about the treatment of rectal cancer. It is intended as a resource to inform and assist clinicians in the care of their patients. It does not provide formal guidelines or recommendations for making health care decisions.</p>

6429</section>

6430<section id="_AboutThis_4">

6431<h3 id="_AboutThis_4_toc">

6432Reviewers and Updates</h3>

6433<p id="_AboutThis_5" tabindex="-1">

6434This summary is reviewed regularly and updated as necessary by the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq/editorial-boards/adult-treatment" title="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq/editorial-boards/adult-treatment">

6435PDQ Adult Treatment Editorial Board</a>

6436, which is editorially independent of the National Cancer Institute (NCI). The summary reflects an independent review of the literature and does not represent a policy statement of NCI or the National Institutes of Health (NIH).</p>

6437<p id="_AboutThis_22" tabindex="-1">

6438 Board members review recently published articles each month to determine whether an article should:</p>

6439<div class="pdq-content-list">

6440<ul id="_AboutThis_6">

6441<li>

6442be discussed at a meeting,</li>

6443<li>

6444be cited with text, or</li>

6445<li>

6446replace or update an existing article that is already cited.</li>

6447</ul>

6448</div>

6449<p id="_AboutThis_7" tabindex="-1">

6450Changes to the summaries are made through a consensus process in which Board members evaluate the strength of the evidence in the published articles and determine how the article should be included in the summary.</p>

6451<p id="" tabindex="-1">

6452The lead reviewers for Rectal Cancer Treatment are:</p>

6453<div class="pdq-content-list">

6454<ul id="">

6455<li>

6456Russell S. Berman, MD (New York University School of Medicine)</li>

6457<li>

6458Amit Chowdhry, MD, PhD (University of Rochester Medical Center)</li>

6459<li>

6460Valerie Lee, MD (Johns Hopkins University)</li>

6461<li>

6462Leon Pappas, MD, PhD (Dana-Farber Cancer Institute)</li>

6463</ul>

6464</div>

6465<p id="_AboutThis_9" tabindex="-1">

6466Any comments or questions about the summary content should be submitted to Cancer.gov through the NCI website's <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/email-us" title="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/email-us">

6467Email Us</a>

6468. Do not contact the individual Board Members with questions or comments about the summaries. Board members will not respond to individual inquiries.</p>

6469</section>

6470<section id="_AboutThis_10">

6471<h3 id="_AboutThis_10_toc">

6472Levels of Evidence</h3>

6473<p id="_AboutThis_11" tabindex="-1">

6474Some of the reference citations in this summary are accompanied by a level-of-evidence designation. These designations are intended to help readers assess the strength of the evidence supporting the use of specific interventions or approaches. The PDQ Adult Treatment Editorial Board uses a <a href="/publications/pdq/levels-evidence/treatment">

6475formal evidence ranking system</a>

6476 in developing its level-of-evidence designations.</p>

6477</section>

6478<section id="_AboutThis_12">

6479<h3 id="_AboutThis_12_toc">

6480Permission to Use This Summary</h3>

6481<p id="_AboutThis_13" tabindex="-1">

6482PDQ is a registered trademark. Although the content of PDQ documents can be used freely as text, it cannot be identified as an NCI PDQ cancer information summary unless it is presented in its entirety and is regularly updated. However, an author would be permitted to write a sentence such as &#8220;NCI&#8217;s PDQ cancer information summary about breast cancer prevention states the risks succinctly: [include excerpt from the summary].&#8221;</p>

6483<p id="_AboutThis_14" tabindex="-1">

6484The preferred citation for this PDQ summary is:</p>

6485<p id="_AboutThis_15" tabindex="-1">

6486PDQ&#174; Adult Treatment Editorial Board. PDQ Rectal Cancer Treatment. Bethesda, MD: National Cancer Institute. Updated &lt;MM/DD/YYYY&gt;. Available at: <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/types/colorectal/hp/rectal-treatment-pdq" title="https://www.cancer.gov/types/colorectal/hp/rectal-treatment-pdq">

6487https://www.cancer.gov/types/colorectal/hp/rectal-treatment-pdq</a>

6488. Accessed &lt;MM/DD/YYYY&gt;. [PMID: 26389402]</p>

6489<p id="_AboutThis_16" tabindex="-1">

6490Images in this summary are used with permission of the author(s), artist, and/or publisher for use within the PDQ summaries only. Permission to use images outside the context of PDQ information must be obtained from the owner(s) and cannot be granted by the National Cancer Institute. Information about using the illustrations in this summary, along with many other cancer-related images, is available in <a href="https://visualsonline.cancer.gov/" title="https://visualsonline.cancer.gov/">

6491Visuals Online</a>

6492, a collection of over 2,000 scientific images.

6493

6494</p>

6495</section>

6496<section id="_AboutThis_17">

6497<h3 id="_AboutThis_17_toc">

6498Disclaimer</h3>

6499<p id="_AboutThis_18" tabindex="-1">

6500Based on the strength of the available evidence, treatment options may be described as either &#8220;standard&#8221; or &#8220;under clinical evaluation.&#8221; These classifications should not be used as a basis for insurance reimbursement determinations. More information on insurance coverage is available on Cancer.gov on the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/managing-care" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/managing-care">

6501Managing Cancer Care</a>

6502 page.</p>

6503</section>

6504<section id="_AboutThis_20">

6505<h3 id="_AboutThis_20_toc">

6506Contact Us</h3>

6507<p id="_AboutThis_21" tabindex="-1">

6508More information about contacting us or receiving help with the Cancer.gov website can be found on our <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/contact" title="https://www.cancer.gov/contact">

6509Contact Us for Help</a>

6510 page. Questions can also be submitted to Cancer.gov through the website&#8217;s <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/email-us" title="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/email-us">

6511Email Us</a>

6512.</p>
